Nowadays , public transport has ended a more price .
The idea of praving public transportation aside is widely supported in developed countries , but the issue is ernected in developing countries , like the one I live in .
As a matter of fact , car ownershgip has increased over the last decade , reducing the number of people using public transport .
The possibility of travelling in your own car is much more convenient than going by a bus full of people or , even worse , the idea of wasting time on a long trip abroad .
Nevertheless , you have another side to this reality .
There are people who can not afford to have their own cars or maybe they can afford to travel by any other means of transportation than the ones provided by the local government .
There are countries where car is so expensive that people choose to pay the the gee rather than pay for a full day .
Similarly , people in countries with less income return to these services because it is a way to reduce their overall expenses .
To conclude , the future of public transport will depend on the usage people use it .
There will be countries in which there will be no need for it , in others where they will need it as long as their economy needs it .
People are easy , fast and vneao solutions .
In general , using a car is easier than taking a train or a bus .
It 's just near your house or your office .
You do n't have to go to a station by walking , gaining weight , or suffering because of the sun or the snow .
But if you are sleepy , tired , bored , or simply you do n't like to drive , you can find sure to take public transport .
And also more enjoyable : you can relax listening to music and looking around , or reading newspapers and books .
Is the car faster than public transport ?
It depends .
The traffic can affect cars and bikes at the same level .
Sometimes cars are faster than buses , sometimes buses are fast .
psedr reasons are always great .
Speaking about money ? Travelling by car seems cheaper than public transport .
But , if we consider all the expenses ( buying the car , paying the insurance , etc . ) , modern cars are not so cheap .
In fact , in every product there are pros and cos .
What about the environment and the quality of life in the cities ?
Public transport is absolutely better .
So , even if travelling by car can not be vonvemiejt at a personal level , public transport has to be preferred by good citizens and strongly shpportwd by yovsrnmjents .
